 uttar pradesh special task force (estf) ke petrol pump sanchaalkon dwaara remote or chip ke jariye eendhan chori ke khulaase ke baad rojaanaa chhapemari main bade paimaane par mashiinon main gadabadi ke maamle ujagar ho rahe hai
 Last night, when the STF team arrived to raid a petrol pump, the entire petrol pump was found missing from there
 pump maalikon ne chaape se bachane ke liye petrol pump kii sari dispencing mashiinon ko ukhdvakar petrol pump ke peeche rakhwa diya or sadak par ek board laga diya jisamen likhaa tha, 'under renovation
 ' lekin estf ne jab ukhaadi gai mashiinon ko khol kar visheshgyon se jaanch karai to pataa chalaa kii unamem eendhan chori ke liye lagi electronic chip nikaal lee gai thi, lekin visheshgyon ko chip lagi hone ke saboot mil gaye
 Investigation revealed that the petrol pump owners had not taken approval from the oil company for renovation of the pump
 rinovations to keval chaape se bachane ke liye kiya ja rahaa tha
 Let us tell you that on April 27 in Lucknow, STF busted the country's largest racket of stealing oil by putting chips in dispensing machines of petrol pumps
 pakad gaye shaks ne kabool kiya tha ki usne tamaam petrol panpon par tel chori kii ek hazaar chip lagaai hai
 On pressing the remote, the meter on the petrol dispensing machine runs at the same speed, but the nozzle leaves less oil
 pakade gaye shaks kii pahchaan par estf ne 7 petrol pump sil kar telchori ke aarope main 23 logon ko giraftaar kiya, jinamein 4 petrol pump maalik bhi shaamil hai
 According to STF, 50 to 100 ml of oil is stolen in one liter
 estf kaa andaja he ki ek chip se petrol chori karne vaala petrol pump ek maheene main 12 se 15 lakh rupee kaa petrol chori kar letaa he
 Similarly, in a year, theft of oil worth about 150 crore rupees from 100 petrol pumps is done only by applying one person's chip
 uttar pradesh main 6000 petrol pump hai jinamein kareeb 60,000 nojal hai
 The arrested person claims that about 90 per cent of petrol pumps perform ghatauli
 tippaniyan The three petrol pumps raided by the STF in Lucknow have found that oil shortages have been reported
 sitapur road par standard petrol pump kii teen mashiinon main gadabadi mili he
 While raiding the Lucknow filling station in Thakurganj area of old Lucknow, there was a report of stealing oil in three machines through a remote
 petrol pump ke prabandhak harikishan verma ne bataaya ki ve subah aate hi remote chaalu kar dete hai taaki kisi ko bhi puraa tel naa mil paae
 Verma said that the chip makers also periodically check the machines, as soon as the machine starts delivering all the oil, immediately the complaint is made and either the chip or its remote is replaced
 verma ne yahaan tak kaha ki ve bahut imaanadaar hai
 They have 24 nozzles here but only three are stealing petrol
 ab estf ne inke khilaaf report darj karne ke baad sabhi ko jail bhejne kii taiyaari kar lee he
 But when the STF opened the dismantled machines and got the experts examined, it was found that the electronic chip for fuel theft was removed in them, but the experts found evidence of the chip being installed
 jaanch se pataa chalaa ki petrol pump maaliko ne pump ke rinovations ke liye tel company se manjuuri nahin lee gai thi
 Renovation was done only to avoid raids
 bataa den ki estf ne lakhanu main 27 april ko petrol pump kii dispencing mashiinon main chip lagaakar tel chori karne kaa desh ke sabase bade racket kaa bhandaphod kiya tha
 The caught man confessed that he had planted a thousand stolen oil chips on all petrol pumps
 remote dabaane par petrol dispencing mashin par meter to usee raftaar se chalata he, lekin nojal se tel kam nikalataa he
 On the identity of the arrested person, STF sealed 7 petrol pumps and arrested 23 people, including 4 petrol pump owners, on charges of oil scouring
 estf ke mutabik, ek litre main 50 se 100 emel tak tel chori kiya jaataa he
 STF estimates that a petrol pump stealing petrol from a chip steals petrol worth Rs 12 to 15 lakhs a month
 isi tarah ek saal main 100 petrol pump se kareeb 150 karod rupee ke tel kii chori to keval ek shaks kii chip lagane se hoti he
 Uttar Pradesh has 6000 petrol pumps with around 60,000 nozzles
 pakade gaye shaks kaa daawa he ki lagbhag 90 fisadi petrol pump ghatatauli karte hai
 The comments estf ne lakhanu main jin teen petrol panpon par chhapemari kii unamem tel kam dene kii baat pataa chali he
 On Sitapur Road, three standard petrol pump machines have found disturbances
 puraane lakhanu ke thakurganj ilaake main lakhanu philing stesan par chhapemari hui to vahaan teen mashiinon main remote ke jariye tel chori karne kii baat saamne ai
 Harikishan Verma, the manager of the petrol pump, said that they turn on the remote as soon as the morning comes so that no one can get all the oil

 According to the Meteorological Department, snowfall and rain in Kashmir will continue for a few more days
 kashmir main paanch maah ke sookhe ke baad gulmarg, pahalgam, sonmarg or to jammu kii patnitop jaise kai unchai vaale sthanon main jahaan barfbaari hui he, vahiin maidani ilaakon main barish hui he
 This has suddenly reduced the temperature significantly
 logon ke liye ye raahat vaali baat isliye bhi he ki kareeb chaar dashak main yah pehali baar hua ki kashmir main paanch maah tak barfbaari nahin hui
 In this case, a wave of happiness has run from the snowfall to the local businessmen
 kashmir main chaaron ore bichhi hui barf kii safed chadar, deodaar tathaa chid ke pedo se girte barf ke tukade yahaan aane waalon ko nai duniya kaa abhas dete hai
 Just look where the snow is, and people see snow playing on it
 mausam vibhaag kii maane to kashmir main barfbaari or barish abhi kuch din or jari rahegi

 It is worth mentioning that the Hindu Yuva Vahini was formed in 2002 by Yogi Adityanath
 tippaniyan According to a report by The Indian Express, Sunil Singh, the provincial president of the Hindu Yuva Vahini, has said that the BJP has insulted the founder of the organization, Yogi Adityanath
 unhone kaha ki purvi uttar pradesh ke log chaahate the ki bijepi, yogi adityanath ko rajya ke mukhyamantri ke chehre ke rup main pesh kare lekin party ne aisa nahin kiya

 iske saath hi unhone joda ki adityanath ne chunaav ke liye 10 pratyaashiyon kii suchi di thi, lekin bijepi ne unamem se keval do hi logon ko tikat diya
